If you do not have one, you can create a Figma account at www.figma.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Figma to Make\n\nTo connect your Figma account to Make follow the general instructions for Connecting to services.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the Figma website where you will be prompted to grant Make access to your account.\n\nConfirm the dialog by clicking the Allow Access button.\n\nActions\nPost a Comment\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Projects\nSearches\nList Comments\nList File Version History\nList Project Files\nList Projects\nFigma\nGetting Started with Figma\nConnecting Figma to Make\nActions\nPost a Comment\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Projects\nSearches\nList Comments\nList File Version History\nList Project Files\nList Projects\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingFacebook Pages\nFacebook Pages\nGetting Started with Facebook Pages\n\nThe Facebook Pages modules allow you to monitor, publish or update posts, photos and videos in your Facebook account.\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Facebook account\n\nA Facebook page you are an admin of\n\nIn order to use Facebook Pages with Make, it is necessary to have a Facebook account. If you do not have one, you can create a Facebook account at facebook.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnect Facebook Account to Make\n\nTo connect Facebook Pages to Make you must connect your Facebook account to Make. To do so, follow the general instructions for Connecting an application.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the Facebook website where you will be prompted to grant Make access to your account.\n\n1. Select the Facebook Pages you want to connect to Make and continue by clicking on the Next button.\n\n2. Allow Make to manage your Facebook Pages and click the Done button.\n\n3. The connection has been established. Confirm and close the dialog by clicking the Ok button.\n\nNote\n\nYou can also follow other pages. You only need to enter a Page ID of the page you want to follow. The following modules are now supported:\n\nList Posts\n\nList Photos\n\nList Videos\n\nWatch Posts\n\nWatch Videos\n\nWatch Photos\n\nGet a Video\n\nGet Post Reactions\n\nGet a Post\n\nGet a Photo\n\nPosts\nWatch Posts\n\nRetrieves the details of new posts when they are added to your page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account.\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to monitor for new posts.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of posts Make will return during one cycle.\n\nWatch Posts (public page)\n\nRetrieves the details of new posts when they are added to a publicly accessible page page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account.\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSpecify or map the public account you want to watch for new posts. The account identification is on the end of the Facebook page URL.\n\nFor example, for the Make HQ account on the URL https://www.facebook.com/itsMakeHQ use itsMakeHQ\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of posts Make will return during one cycle.\n\nList Posts\n\nLists posts from the selected Facebook page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve posts from.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of posts Make will return during one cycle.\n\nGet a Post\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve the post from.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the post you want to retrieve details about.\n\nGet Post Reactions\n\nReturns the total count of selected reactions (LIKE, LOVE, WOW, HAHA, SAD, ANGRY).\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve the post reactions from.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the post you want to retrieve the reactions from.\n\n\n\n\nType\n\n\t\n\nSelect the type of reaction you want to retrieve. If left blank, all reactions will be counted.\n\nCreate a Post\n\nCreates a post on your Facebook page and returns its Post ID.\n\nPermissions may need to be extended in order to create a post on your Facebook page.\n\n1. Click on the Continue button.\n\n2. Extend the permission by clicking on the OK button.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page where you want to create a post.\n\n\n\n\nMessage\n\n\t\n\nEnter the post's text content.\n\n\n\n\nLink\n\n\t\n\nEnter the link that will be attached to the post if needed.\n\nUpdate a Post\n\nAllows you to update a post's message.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page where you want to update a post.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the post you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nMessage\n\n\t\n\nEnter a new post's text content.\n\nDelete a Post\n\nDeletes a post from the Facebook page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to delete a post from.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the post you want to delete.\n\nLike a Post\n\nAdds a like to the post.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page where you want to like a post.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the post you want to add a like to.\n\nUnlike a Post\n\nDeletes a like from the post.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page where you want to delete a like.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the post you want to delete a like from.\n\nVideos\nWatch Videos\n\nTriggers when a new video is added to the Facebook page and retrieves its details.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to watch for new videos.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of videos Make will return during one cycle.\n\nList Videos\n\nRetrieves a list of videos from the selected Facebook page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve the videos from.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of videos Make will return during one cycle.\n\nGet a Video\n\nRetrieves the details of a specified video.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve the video from.\n\n\n\n\nVideo ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Video ID of the video you want to retrieve information about.\n\nUpload a Video\n\nUploads a video to the Facebook page.\n\nSupported video formats are: 3g2, 3gp, 3gpp, asf, avi, dat, divx, dv, f4v, flv, gif, m2ts, m4v, mkv, mod, mov, mp4, mpe, mpeg, mpeg4, mpg, mts, nsv, ogm, ogv, qt, tod, ts, vob, and wmv.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page where you want to upload a video to.\n\n\n\n\nSource file\n\n\t\n\nMap the file you want to upload. For more detailed information refer to the Working with files article.\n\n\n\n\nTitle\n\n\t\n\nEnter the video's title.\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter the description for the video.\n\nWarning\n\nThe description must not contain numbers otherwise the video will not be published and the message Your post goes against our community standards so only you can see it will be returned. In order to add numbers to the description use the Facebook Pages > Update a Video module.\n\nUpdate a Video\n\nAllows you to update a title and description of the video on the Facebook page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page where you want to upload a video to.\n\n\n\n\nVideo ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Video ID of the video you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nTitle\n\n\t\n\nEnter the video's title.\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter the description for the video.\n\nDelete Video\n\nDeletes the selected video.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to delete a video from.\n\n\n\n\nVideo ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Video ID of the video you want to delete.\n\nPhotos\nWatch Photos\n\nRetrieves the details of new photos when they are added to the page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to watch for new videos.\n\n\n\n\nAlbum\n\n\t\n\nSelect the album you want to watch for new photos.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of photos Make will return during one cycle.\n\nList Photos\n\nRetrieves the details of photos from a specified album.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve the photos from.\n\n\n\n\nAlbum\n\n\t\n\nSelect the album you want to retrieve photos from.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of photos Make will return during one cycle.\n\nGet a Photo\n\nRetrieves the details of a specified photo.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve the photo from.\n\n\n\n\nPhoto ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Photo ID of the video you want to retrieve information about.\n\nUpload a Photo\n\nUploads a photo to the Facebook page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page where you want to upload a photo.\n\n\n\n\nAlbum\n\n\t\n\nSelect the album you want to upload a photo to.\n\n\n\n\nSource file\n\n\t\n\nMap the file you want to upload. For more detailed information refer to the Working with files article.\n\n\n\n\nMessage\n\n\t\n\nEnter the text message that will be posted together with the photo in one post.\n\nDelete a Photo\n\nDeletes the selected photo.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to delete a photo from.\n\n\n\n\nPhoto ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Photo ID of the photo you want to delete.\n\nComments\nWatch Comments\n\nTriggers when a new comment is added to the Facebook page's post and retrieves its details.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to watch for new comments.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the post you want to watch for new comments.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of comments Make will return during one cycle.\n\nList Comments\n\nReturns a post's comments.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to list the post's comments from.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the post you want to get the comments from.\n\n\n\n\nFilter\n\n\t\n\nStream\n\nRetrieves all comments (including replies to the comment)\n\nOnly top level comments\n\nRetrieves top level comments, without its replies.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of comments Make will return during one cycle.\n\nGet a Comment\n\nRetrieves a comment.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to get a post comment from.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the post you want to retrieve the comment from.\n\nCreate a Comment\n\nAdds a comment to the selected post on behalf of the page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to create the post's comment at.\n\n\n\n\nPost ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the post you want to comment.\n\n\n\n\nMessage\n\n\t\n\nEnter the text for the comment.\n\n\n\n\nAttachment type\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to attach a photo file [JPG, PNG, etc.] or a GIF file. The URL must link directly to the desired image file.\n\nDelete a Comment\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to delete the post's comment from.\n\n\n\n\nComment ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the comment you want to delete.\n\nPage\nGet Page Info\n\nRetrieves the details of a selected page.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook account\n\n\n\n\nPage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the page you want to retrieve details from.\n\nTroubleshooting\nThe Make dropdown doesn't show some Facebook Pages:\n\nIf some of your pages are not available in the Make modules please follow the steps below:\n\n1. Open the Facebook Settings and click on Business Integrations or use this link https://www.facebook.com/settings?tab=business_tools\n\n2. Open the Make app\n\n3. Check off all of the pages you want to see in the Make modules:\n\n4. Save the changes by clicking the Save button.\n\nFacebook Pages\nGetting Started with Facebook Pages\nConnect Facebook Account to Make\nPosts\nWatch Posts\nWatch Posts (public page)\nList Posts\nGet a Post\nGet Post Reactions\nCreate a Post\nUpdate a Post\nDelete a Post\nLike a Post\nUnlike a Post\nVideos\nWatch Videos\nList Videos\nGet a Video\nUpload a Video\nUpdate a Video\nDelete Video\nPhotos\nWatch Photos\nList Photos\nGet a Photo\nUpload a Photo\nDelete a Photo\nComments\nWatch Comments\nList Comments\nGet a Comment\nCreate a Comment\nDelete a Comment\nPage\nGet Page Info\nTroubleshooting\nThe Make dropdown doesn't show some Facebook Pages:\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

(2650, OAuthException )\n\nReason: Facebook Custom Audiences won't let Make add emails or users unless the Custom Audience were created by Make. This error indicates that the selected Custom Audience wasn't created by Make, but by another platform or via manual upload.\n\nSolution:\n\nCreate a custom audience from Make using Create Custom Audience or other modules using a scenario.\n\nNow go back to your previous scenario, and add your member to that newly created custom audience.\n\nIf you continue to receive this response, you may need to accept Facebook Custom Audience Terms and Condition in each of your ad accounts. If you do not have one, you can create an Elastic Email account at elasticemail.com/account#/create-account.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Elastic Email to Make\n\nTo connect your Elastic Email account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Elastic Email account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your Elastic Email account.\n\nClick Your User Name > Settings > API > Accept Consent > Create API Key. Enter a name for the key, select the permissions, and click Create. Copy the API key to your clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the Elastic Email module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied in step 2.\n\nSelect whether you want to establish the connection for private branding and enter the custom domain. For example, <yourdomain.cz(uk, etc.)>. You can find at My Account > Settings > Domains.\n\nClick Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nContacts\nWatch Contact Added to the List\nCreate a Contact\nGet a Contact\nUpdate a Contact\nDelete a Contact\nSearch Contacts\nUnsubscribe a Contact\nLists\nCreate a List\nGet a List\nUpdate a List\nDelete a List\nSearch Lists\nCampaigns\nWatch Campaign Sent\nEmails\nSend an Email\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Lists\nElastic Email\nGetting Started with Elastic Email\nConnecting Elastic Email to Make\nContacts\nWatch Contact Added to the List\nCreate a Contact\nGet a Contact\nUpdate a Contact\nDelete a Contact\nSearch Contacts\nUnsubscribe a Contact\nLists\nCreate a List\nGet a List\nUpdate a List\nDelete a List\nSearch Lists\nCampaigns\nWatch Campaign Sent\nEmails\nSend an Email\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Lists\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create an Emercury account on the Emercury website.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Emercury to Make\n\nTo connect your Emercury account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your account.\n\nLog into your Emercury account.\n\nClick on the cogwheel in the top-right corner and select the API Keys option from the menu.\n\nRequest your API Key by clicking the REQUEST API button.\n\nOnce your request is approved the displayed page will contain the API Key.\n\nCopy the provided API key.\n\nGo to Make and open the Emercury module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nEnter the email address that you created your Emercury account with into the User Email Address field.\n\nEnter the API Key you have copied in step 5 to the respective field and click the Continue button.\n\nThe connection is now established and you can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nEmercury\nGetting Started with Emercury\nConnecting Emercury to Make\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

User names you can select from will display as you type.\n\n\n\n\nGlobal Key (allows all actions)\n\n\t\n\nEnable this option to allow all actions. Otherwise, define the particular scopes you want to enable for the API access.\n\nClick Save, and copy the provided API Key.\n\nGo to Make, and open the Discourse module's Create a connection dialog. Fill in the following fields:\n\nConnection name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the connection to your Discourse account.\n\n\n\n\nHost URL\n\n\t\n\nSelect the URL of your Discourse domain name (including HTTPS), for example, https://<yourCompanyName>.trydiscourse.com.\n\n\n\n\nAPI Key\n\n\t\n\nEnter the API Key you have copied in Step 6 above.\n\n\n\n\nAPI User Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user name of the user assigned to the API Key.\n\nClick Save.\n\nThe connection has been established. You can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nBuild Discourse Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nWatch Posts Events\n\nWatch Posts\n\nWatch Solved Events\n\nWatch Like Events\n\nLike Posts\n\nGet a Post\n\nCreate a Post. Topic, or Private Message\n\nUpdate a Post\n\nDelete a Post\n\nWatch Topic Events\n\nWatch Topics\n\nList Topics\n\nUpdate a Topic\n\nDelete a Topic\n\nWatch Private Messages\n\nList Private Messages\n\nWatch Group Events\n\nWatch Group User Events\n\nWatch Category Events\n\nWatch Tag Events\n\nWatch Reviewable Events\n\nWatch Notication Events\n\nWatch Badge Grant EVents\n\nMake an API Call\n\nDiscourse\nConnecting Discourse to Make\nBuild Discourse Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a Delesign account at delesign.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting to Delesign to Make\n\nTo connect your Delesign account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Delesign account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your Delesign account and open your Dashboard.\n\nClick Integrations > Delesign API.\n\nCopy the API Token to your clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the Delesign module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Token field, enter the token copied in step 3, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nProjects\nSearch Projects\nGets a Project\nCreate a Project\nUpdate a Project\nDelete a Project\nMessage\nCreate a Message\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Projects\nDelesign\nGetting Started with Delesign\nConnecting to Delesign to Make\nProjects\nSearch Projects\nGets a Project\nCreate a Project\nUpdate a Project\nDelete a Project\nMessage\nCreate a Message\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Projects\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a ConvertKit account at app.convertkit.com/users/signup.\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting ConvertKit to Make\n\nTo connect your ConvertKit account to Make you need to obtain the API Secret from your ConvertKit account.\n\n1. Log in to your ConvertKit account.\n\n2. Open the Account settings.\n\n3. Click the Show button in the API Secret section and copy the displayed API Secret.\n\n4. Go to the Make ConvertKit module and open the Create a connection dialog.\n\n5. Enter the API Secret to the respective field and click the Continue button.\n\nNow you can proceed with setting up the ConvertKit module.\n\nAdd a Subscriber to Form\n\nSubscribe subscriber's email address to one of your forms.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nForm ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the form you want to add the subscriber to.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the subscriber's email address.\n\n\n\n\nFirst name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the first name of the subscriber.\n\n\n\n\nTag\n\n\t\n\nSelect the tag you want add to the subscriber.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Fields\n\n\t\n\nEnter values for the custom fields.\n\nThe custom field must be created in the ConvertKit UI before it is displayed in the module.\n\nList Form Subscribers\n\nLists form subscribers.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nForm ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Form ID of the form you want to list subscribers from.\n\n\n\n\nOrder\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to sort the result in ascending or descending order.\n\n\n\n\nSubscriber State\n\n\t\n\nSet whether you want to return active subscribers or canceled subscribers only.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nThe maximum number of subscribers Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nList Subscribers\n\nReturns a list of your subscribers.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nFilter results by the subscriber's email address.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nThe maximum number of subscribers Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\n\n\n\nAdded on or after\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date to filter subscribers added on or after this date. Use the YYYY-MM-DD format.\n\n\n\n\nAdded on or before\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date to filter subscribers added on or before this date. Use the YYYY-MM-DD format.\n\n\n\n\nUpdated from\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date to filter subscribers who have been updated after this date. Use the YYYY-MM-DD format.\n\n\n\n\nUpdated to\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date to filter subscribers who have been updated before this date. Use the YYYY-MM-DD format.\n\nGet a Subscriber\n\nReturns the details of a single subscriber.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nSubscriber ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Subscriber ID of the subscriber you want to retrieve information about.\n\nUpdate a Subscriber\n\nUpdates details of a single subscriber.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nSubscriber ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Subscriber ID of the subscriber whose details you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the subscriber's email address that you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nFirst name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the first name of the subscriber you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Fields\n\n\t\n\nEnter the value for the desired custom fields.\n\nUnsubscribe a Subscriber\n\nUnsubscribe subscriber's email address from all your forms and sequences.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the email of the subscriber you want to unsubscribe.\n\nWatch Subscriber Activated\n\nTriggers when a subscriber is activated.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook. E.g. Subscriber Activated.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\nWatch Form Subscriptions\n\nTriggers when a new subscription is submitted.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook. E.g. New Form Subscription.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nForm ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the form you want to monitor for new subscriptions.\n\nSequences\nAdd a Subscriber to Sequence\n\nSubscribes an email address to one of your sequences.\n\nIf the new email address is entered, the new subscriber will be created.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nSequences ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the sequence you want to add the subscriber to.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the subscriber's email address.\n\n\n\n\nFirst name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the first name of the subscriber you want to add to the sequence.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Fields\n\n\t\n\nEnter values for the custom fields.\n\nThe custom field must be created in the ConvertKit UI before it is displayed in the module.\n\n\n\n\nTags\n\n\t\n\nAdd tags for the new subscriber.\n\nList Sequence Subscribers\n\nLists subscriptions to a sequence including subscriber data.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nSequences ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the sequence you want to list subscribers from.\n\n\n\n\nOrder\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to sort the result in ascending or descending order.\n\n\n\n\nSubscriber state\n\n\t\n\nSet whether you want to return active subscribers or canceled subscribers only.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nThe maximum number of subscribers Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nTags\nAdd a Tag to a Subscriber\n\nAdds a tag to a subscriber.\n\nWhen a new email is specified, the new subscriber will be created.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nTag ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the tag you want to assign to the subscriber.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the subscriber's email address. Subscribe an email address to a tag to have that tag applied to the subscriber with that email address.\n\n\n\n\nFirst Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the first name of the subscriber.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Fields\n\n\t\n\nEnter values for the custom fields.\n\nThe custom field must be created in the ConvertKit UI before it is displayed in the module.\n\nRemove a Tag by ID\n\nRemoves a tag from a subscriber.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nSubscriber ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Subscriber ID of the subscriber you want to remove the tag from. The Subscriber ID can be retrieved, for example, using the List Subscribers, or List Subscribers by Tag modules.\n\n\n\n\nTag ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the tag you want to remove from the subscriber.\n\nRemove a Tag by Email\n\nRemoves a tag from a subscriber by email.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail Address\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the email address of the subscriber you want to remove the tag from. The subscriber's email address can be retrieved, for example, using the List Subscribers, or List Subscribers by Tag modules.\n\n\n\n\nTag ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the tag you want to remove from the subscriber.\n\nList Subscribers by Tag\n\nRetrieves all subscribers that are tagged by a specified tag.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nTag ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the tag you want to list the subscribers by.\n\n\n\n\nOrder\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to sort the result in ascending or descending order.\n\n\n\n\nSubscriber state\n\n\t\n\nSet whether you want to return active subscribers only or canceled subscribers only.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nThe maximum number of subscribers Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nGet Subscribers Tags\n\nLists all the tags assigned to a subscriber.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nSubscriber ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Subscriber ID of the subscriber you want to retrieve tags from.\n\nThe Subscriber ID can be retrieved, for example, using the List Subscribers, or List Subscribers by Tag modules.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nThe maximum number of tags Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nWatch Tag Added\n\nTriggers when a selected tag is added to a subscriber and returns subscriber's details.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook. E.g. New Tag Added.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nTag ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the tag you want to monitor for new additions.\n\nWatch Tag Removed\n\nTriggers when a selected tag is removed from a subscriber and returns subscriber's details.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook. E.g. New Tag Added.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nTag ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the tag you want to monitor for removal.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nAllows you to perform a custom API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your ConvertKit account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.convertkit.com. E.g. /v3/subscribers\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the ConvertKit API v3 documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGETto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOSTto create a new entry.\n\nPUTto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCHto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETEto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Subscribers\n\nThe following API call returns all subscribers:\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > subscribers.In our example, 3 subscribers were returned:\n\nConvertKit\nGetting Started with ConvertKit\nConnecting ConvertKit to Make\nAdd a Subscriber to Form\nList Form Subscribers\nList Subscribers\nGet a Subscriber\nUpdate a Subscriber\nUnsubscribe a Subscriber\nWatch Subscriber Activated\nWatch Form Subscriptions\nSequences\nAdd a Subscriber to Sequence\nList Sequence Subscribers\nTags\nAdd a Tag to a Subscriber\nRemove a Tag by ID\nRemove a Tag by Email\nList Subscribers by Tag\nGet Subscribers Tags\nWatch Tag Added\nWatch Tag Removed\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Subscribers\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Create an account on www.clickfunnels.com.\n\nAn already built funnel. More information about building your first funnel.\n\nAn established connection to ClickFunnels using a webhook.\n\nWatch the ClickFunnels integration video\nCreating a New Funnel Webhook\n\n1. Create an Make webhook and copy the provided link.\n\n2. Open the Settings in the funnel that you want to process data from.\n\n3. Click the Manage Your Funnel Webhooks button at the bottom of the Settings page.\n\n4. Click on the New Webhook button.\n\n5. Paste the Make webhook in the URL field.\n\n6. Select the event you want to watch.\n\n7. Click on the green button, CREATE FUNNEL WEBHOOK\n\nIf you select more events, for example, \"purchase created\" and \"purchase updated\" your webhook module (in Make) will be triggered twice after any new purchase.\n\nImportant to know:\n\nClickFunnels sends webhooks from each page. Even though it's only transferred to the next step, the action on the button says Submit Form. So, what happens if you use this button on different pages? ClickFunnels submits the form again, even though the event calls for creating a contact.\n\nThe solution for this is to put a filter to filter by page ID (placing the filter after the ClickFunnels' webhook module in Make) you can notice that duplicated webhooks come from another page with different ID:\n\nFilter example:\n\nTriggers\nWatch new contacts\n\nIf a new contact is created in the funnel then this module reads its data. The data can be further processed in the Make scenario.\n\nTo run this module, you need to add a webhook to the desired funnel.\n\nWatch new purchases\n\nRetrieves purchase data (product details, contact details, amount, etc.) when a new purchase is made.\n\nTo run this module, you need to add a webhook to the desired funnel.\n\nSample scenarios\n\nYou can find sample scenario templates with ClickFunnels modules here, www.make.com/en/templates/click-funnels.\n\nActions\nAdd Contact\n\nAdds a contact to a specified ClickFunnels page.\n\nPage URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter the required ClickFunnels page URL.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the new contact entry.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email of the new contact entry.\n\nClickFunnels\nGetting Started with ClickFunnels\nPrerequisites\nWatch the ClickFunnels integration video\nCreating a New Funnel Webhook\nImportant to know:\nTriggers\nSample scenarios\nActions\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a Buffer account at buffer.com/pricing/publish.\n\nCaution\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Buffer to Make\n\n1. Go to Make and open the Buffer module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n2. Enter the name of the connection to the Connection name field and click Continue.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the Buffer website where you will be prompted to grant Make access to your account.\n\nConfirm the dialog by clicking the Allow access button.\n\nActions\nCreate a status update\n\nCreates a new status update in the specified services.\n\nNote\n\nA status update represents a single post to a single social media account.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Buffer account.\n\n\n\n\nProfiles\n\n\t\n\nSelect profiles the status update should be sent to.\n\n\n\n\nText\n\n\t\n\nEnter the text content of the status update.\n\n\n\n\nPublication\n\n\t\n\nSelect when the update should be posted.\n\nPost immediately\n\nPosts the status update now (when the module is executed) to all profiles instead of being added to the buffer.\n\nAdd an update to the top of the queue\n\nThe update will be added to the top of the buffer and will become the next update sent.\n\nPost an update at a scheduled date and time\n\nEnter the date and time to the Date scheduled field. The list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nAttach media to the update\n\n\t\n\nSpecify the media you want to attach to the update.\n\nLink\n\n\t\n\nEnter the direct link to the image.\n\n\n\n\nTitle\n\n\t\n\nEnter the title of the update status.\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter the description of the update status.\n\n\n\n\nLink to an image\n\n\t\n\nEnter the URL of the image. The image will be uploaded to Facebook.\n\n\n\n\nThumbnail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the URL of the thumbnail of the image specified above.\n\n\n\n\nShorten links in the text as media\n\n\t\n\nIf left disabled (unchecked), links within the text will not be automatically shortened, otherwise, they will.\n\n\n\n\nAttach links in the text as media\n\n\t\n\nIf there are links in the text field, they will be attached to the post as media.\n\nUpdate a status update\n\nUpdates an existing post.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Buffer account.\n\n\n\n\nUpdate ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Status ID (mapped from the Create a status page module) of the status update you want to update.\n\nThe update status you want to update must not be posted. Only update statuses that haven't been published yet can be updated.\n\n\n\n\nText\n\n\t\n\nEnter the text content of the status update.\n\n\n\n\nPublication\n\n\t\n\nSelect when the update should be posted.\n\nPost immediately\n\nPosts the status update now (when the module is executed) to all profiles instead of being added to the buffer.\n\nPost an update at a scheduled date and time\n\nEnter the date and time to the Date scheduled field. The list of supported date and time formats.\n\nDelete Status\n\nDeletes a status update.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Buffer account.\n\n\n\n\nUpdate ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Status ID (mapped from the Create a status page module) of the status update you want to delete.\n\nThe update status you want to update must not be posted. Only update statuses that haven't been published yet can be updated.\n\nBuffer\nGetting Started with Buffer\nConnecting Buffer to Make\nActions\nCreate a status update\nUpdate a status update\nDelete Status\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can now edit your scenario and add more Brevo modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Brevo Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nContacts\n\nWatch Contacts\n\nList Contacts\n\nList Lists in a Folder\n\nList Contacts in a List\n\nGet a Contact\n\nAdd Existing Contacts to a List\n\nCreate a Contact\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nDelete a Contact\n\nLists\n\nWatch Lists\n\nList Lists\n\nGet a List\n\nCreate a List\n\nUpdate a List\n\nDelete a List\n\nFolders\n\nWatch Folders\n\nList Folders\n\nGet a Folder\n\nCreate a Folder\n\nUpdate a Folder\n\nDelete a Folder\n\nCampaigns\n\nWatch Email Campaigns\n\nList Email Campaigns\n\nCreate an Email Campaign\n\nGet an Email Campaign\n\nUpdate an Email Campaign\n\nDelete an Email Campaign\n\nOther\n\nNew Event\n\nSend an SMS\n\nSend an Email\n\nSend a Campaign Report\n\nMake an API Call\n\nGet My Account\n\nBrevo\nConnect Brevo to Make\nBuild Brevo Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a BigMarker account at www.bigmarker.com/signup.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting BigMarker to Make\n\nTo connect your BigMarker account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your BigMarker account.\n\nLog in to your BigMarker account.\n\nClick on your profile icon in the top-right corner and Settings.\n\nOpen the API & White Label settings.\n\nClick Request API Key.\n\nCopy the provided API Key to the clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the BigMarker module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nEnter the API Key you have copied in step 5 to the respective field and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nThe connection has been established. You can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nConferences\nList Future Conferences\nSearch Conferences\nSearch Recurring Conferences\nGet a Conference\nCreate a Conference\nUpdate a Conference\nDelete a Conference\nConference Registrants/Attendees\nList a Conference's Registrants\nRegister a User to a Conference\nUnregister User from a Conference\nList Conference's Attendees\nChannels\nList Channels\nGet a Channel\nList a Channel's Conferences\nList a Channel's Subscribers\nAdd a Channel Subscriber\nDelete a Channel Subscriber\nPresenters\nList a Presenter's Conferences\nAdd a Presenter to a Conference\nUpdate a Conference Presenter\nDelete a Conference Presenter\nMake an API Call\n\nAllows you to perform a custom API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your BigMarker account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://www.bigmarker.com/api.For example: /v1/channels.\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the BigMarker API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET\n\nto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST\n\nto create a new entry.\n\nPUT\n\nto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH\n\nto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE\n\nto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Dashboards\n\nThe following API call returns all dashboards in your XXXXXX account:\n\nURL:\n\nv1/conferences/\n\nMethod:\n\nGET\n\nThe result can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > dashboards.\n\nIn our example, 2 conferences were returned:\n\nBigMarker\nGetting Started with BigMarker\nConnecting BigMarker to Make\nConferences\nList Future Conferences\nSearch Conferences\nSearch Recurring Conferences\nGet a Conference\nCreate a Conference\nUpdate a Conference\nDelete a Conference\nConference Registrants/Attendees\nList a Conference's Registrants\nRegister a User to a Conference\nUnregister User from a Conference\nList Conference's Attendees\nChannels\nList Channels\nGet a Channel\nList a Channel's Conferences\nList a Channel's Subscribers\nAdd a Channel Subscriber\nDelete a Channel Subscriber\nPresenters\nList a Presenter's Conferences\nAdd a Presenter to a Conference\nUpdate a Conference Presenter\nDelete a Conference Presenter\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Dashboards\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

      "title": "RSS",
      "url": "https://www.make.com/en/help/apps/lifestyle/rss",
      "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nAction Network\nFeedly\nInoreader\nPocket\nRSS\nSteam\nStrava\nVirtuagym\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsLifestyleRSS\nRSS\n\nThe RSS modules enable you to monitor and import items from an RSS feed/Atom export of any website.\n\nGetting Started With RSS\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA URL of the RSS feed/Atom export\n\nIn order to use RSS with Make, it is necessary to retrieve a feed URL. Please refer to the How to retrieve the website's feed URL article.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nHow to Retrieve the Website's Feed URL\n\nIf you don't know the RSS/Atom feed URL of the website you want to retrieve a feed from, you can try adding a common RSS feed URL part after the website URL.\n\nCommon feed URLs can be in the following formats: www.website.com/feed or www.website.com/rss.\n\nFor example, https://www.make.com/en/blog/feed or https://www.theguardian.com/uk/technology/rss.\n\nYou can retrieve the RSS feed URL using one of the third-party browser extensions. For example, RSS Subscription Extension (Chrome) or Feedbro (Firefox).\n\nYou can also find the RSS feed URL manually in the website's source code:\n\n1. Open the website you want to retrieve a feed from.\n\n2. Press Ctrl+U (Windows) or Command+Option+U (Mac) on your keyboard to view the page source code.\n\n3. Press Ctrl+F (Windows) or Command+F (Mac) on your keyboard to search the page source code.\n\n4. Search for \"rss\", \"feed\", or \"atom\" to find the RSS feed URL.\n\n5. Copy the URL.\n\nTriggers\nWatch RSS Feed Items\n\nReturns feed item details when a feed item is posted.\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a URL of the RSS or Atom feed.\n\n\n\n\nMaximum number of returned items\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of feed items Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nCaution\n\nIf the value is set too high, the connection may be interrupted on the side of the given third-party service (timeout). Make has no influence on this. We recommend you set a lower value, and either define a higher value for the maximum number of cycles or run the scenario more frequently. For more information, please see the scenario cycles and phases online help page.\n\n\n\n\nUser name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user name if the feed is password-protected.\n\n\n\n\nPassword\n\n\t\n\nEnter the password if the feed is password-protected.\n\n\n\n\nProcess RSS fields\n\n\t\n\nEnable the Google Merchant Center option to process fields from the Google Merchant Center feed.\n\n\n\n\nRequest compressed content\n\n\t\n\nEnable this option to request a compressed version of the website.\n\nActions\nRetrieve RSS Feed Items\n\nRetrieves feed items from the specified URL.\n\nProcess RSS fields\n\n\t\n\nEnable the Google Merchant Center option to process fields from the Google Merchant Center feed.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a URL of the RSS or Atom feed.\n\n\n\n\nUser name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user name if the feed is password-protected.\n\n\n\n\nPassword\n\n\t\n\nEnter the password if the feed is password-protected.\n\n\n\n\nDate from\n\n\t\n\nEnter a date you want to filter returned RSS feed items from. Make will process all items that are more recent than the specified date.\n\n\n\n\nDate to\n\n\t\n\nEnter a date up to which you want to filter returned RSS feed items. Make will process all items dated on or before the specified date.\n\n\n\n\nMaximum number of returned items\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of feed items Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nCaution\n\nIf the value is set too high, the connection may be interrupted on the side of the given third-party service (timeout). Make has no influence on this. We recommend you set a lower value, and either define a higher value for the maximum number of cycles or run the scenario more frequently. For more information, please see the scenario cycles and phases online help page.\n\n\n\n\nRequest compressed content\n\n\t\n\nEnable this option to request a compressed version of the website.\n\nCommon Problems With the Watch RSS Feed Items Trigger\nTrigger Execution Failed\n\nThere are several situations when a trigger execution can terminate with an error.\n\nThe URL you have entered does not exist or does not contain a valid RSS feed/Atom export. If this happens, the scenario will be stopped, and you will need to enter the correct address.\n\nThe RSS/Atom file size exceeds the allowed limit. If this happens, the import will be stopped. For more information, please refer to the Working with files section.\n\nTrigger Did Not Process RSS Feed Items\n\nWith websites that frequently update their RSS feed/Atom export, it can happen that some RSS feed items do not get processed.\n\nHere is an example: A news portal publishes 40 articles every day, but it only includes the last 20 articles in its RSS/Atom export feed. If the interval for processing is set to one day, then Make sees only the last 20 articles. Make does not have access to the previous 20 articles, and therefore, it cannot process them.\n\nIf this is the case, you'll need to set a shorter interval for processing the articles, like every 12 hours.\n\nIf this is not the case, and the article still has not been processed, it may be that the trigger has not yet reached the given article when being executed.\n\nRSS\nGetting Started With RSS\nHow to Retrieve the Website's Feed URL\nTriggers\nWatch RSS Feed Items\nActions\nRetrieve RSS Feed Items\nCommon Problems With the Watch RSS Feed Items Trigger\nTrigger Execution Failed\nTrigger Did Not Process RSS Feed Items\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

For example, the following would not be recognized correctly by Make:\n\n<complexType name=\"ArrayOfFloat\">\n  <complexContent>\n    <restriction base=\"soapenc:Array\">\n      <attribute ref=\"soapenc:arrayType\" wsdl:arrayType=\"xsd:integer[]\"/>    \n    </restriction>  \n  </complexContent>\n</complexType>\n\n\nIt includes the soapenc:Array, soapenc:arrayType and wsdl:arrayType references, which are not yet supported in Make.\n\nRedefine elements\n\nFraction digits restrictions\n\nTotal digits restrictions\n\nWhite space restrictions\n\nMultiple parts in input and output messages. Only single-part messages are supported\n\nWorkaround\n\nIf the SOAP module refuses to process the WSDL file or throws various errors in the module's configuration, you may try using the universal HTTP > Make a request module instead:\n\nIn Make, create a new scenario.\n\nInsert the HTTP > Make a request module in the scenario.\n\nOpen the module's configuration and configure it like shown below:\n\nOpen a new web browser window/tab.\n\nPaste the WSDL URL into the web browser's address bar and fetch the XML file. The WSDL URL usually ends with ?wsdl, but not necessarily, e.g. http://voip.ms/api/v1/server.wsdl\n\nIf the WSDL file does not display directly in the web browser, open the downloaded file in a text editor.\n\nSearch for the <service> or <wsdl:service>tag:\n\nOnce located, copy the URL from the location attribute.\n\nIn Make, paste the URL into the HTTP module's URL field.\n\nOpen the Online SOAP Client in a new web browser window/tab.\n\nPaste the WSDL URL into the WSDL URL field.\n\nClick on the Browse button.\n\nPick from the list of functions to the left, e.g. getLanguages.\n\nCopy the content of the Request XML text area.\n\nIn Make, paste the copied content to the module's Request content field.\n\nProvide values for selected parameters by replacing the question marks with actual values:\n\nClose the module's configuration by clicking on the OK button.\n\nExecute the scenario/module.\n\nSOAP\nSupported features\nWorkaround\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

For subscription information, refer to the Pingdom Pricing page.\n\nRefer to the Pingdom API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Pingdom to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Pingdom.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Pingdom\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Pingdom account:\n\nLog in to your Pingdom account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click the Settings icon > Pingdom API.\n\nClick Add API token.\n\nEnter a name for the token, select Read access, and click Generate token.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Token field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Pingdom in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to yourÂ MakeÂ account, add aÂ Pingdom module to yourÂ scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In theÂ Connection nameÂ field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn theÂ API TokenÂ field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Pingdom modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet Up Pingdom Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd a Pingdom instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nLog in to your Pingdom account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click the Settings icon > Integrations.\n\nClick Add integration.\n\nIn the Name field, enter a name for the webhook.\n\nIn the URL field, paste the webhook URL copied in step 4.\n\nClick Save integration.\n\nPingdom will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild Pingdom Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nTriggers\n\nWatch New Alert\n\nWatch Contacts\n\nWatch Checks\n\nActions\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPingdom\nConnect Pingdom to Make\nObtain your API key in Pingdom\nEstablish the connection with Pingdom in Make\nSet Up Pingdom Webhooks\nBuild Pingdom Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsIT and DevelopmentMustache\nMustache\nGetting Started with Mustache\nPrerequisites\n\nA source of variables that will be used for creating result text using the Mustache template.\n\nWe can use Google Sheets for this purpose.\n\nTo work with Google Sheets, you have to have a Google account. If you do not have one, you can create a Google account at https://accounts.google.com.\n\nMustache\n\nFor more details about the Mustache template system, please visit the Mustache official website.\n\nAdding a Mustache Module to your Scenario\n\n1. Click on the blue button, Create a new scenario in the top-right corner of Makeâs Dashboard page or Scenarios page\n\n2. Search for the Mustache module using the search field\n\n3. Select Mustache by clicking on the module's icon\n\n4. Click on the Continue button\n\n5. Your scenario is now open\n\n6. Start by clicking on the white question mark icon in the center of your scenario\n\n7. Select Mustache from the menu\n\nTransformers\nCompile a Template\n\nMustache is a simple template system allowing you to generate output content from the provided template with variables.\n\nTo demonstrate what the module does, we will generate a short party invitation sent by email.\n\nTemplate\n\n\t\n\nCreate the desired Mustache template in this field. Use variables as required and close them into double curly braces {{}}. These braces are called mustaches.\n\n\n\n\nVariables\n\n\t\n\nNow you have to define the variables used in your text above. We have used four variables in mustaches in our sample template. These variables are name, date, time and place.\n\nSetting Up Variables in the Mustache Module\n\n1. Click on the Add item button in the Variables section\n\n2. There are two fields in the Add item dialog â Key and Value.\n\nKey\n\n\t\n\nEnter a variable used in your template. Do not use curly braces.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nSpecify the source of the variable. We have used the Google Sheets module, Watch a Worksheet trigger and have chosen the Events table from where to load the variables.\n\nWhen someone enters values into the table, these values will be used as variables for our Mustache template.\n\nSetting up a variable in the Mustache module\n\nNow, when the source of variables (using the Google Sheets module) and all needed variables in the Mustache module are set, we should decide what to do with the resulting text we get as output from the Mustache module.\n\nAs an example, we will send an email with our invitation.\n\nSetting up a Target for the Mustache Template\n\nMustache, as a transformer module, cannot be the last in the scenario.\n\n1. Add another module after the Mustache module\n\n2. It can be the Email module, for example\n\n3. Select the Send an email action\n\nSend an email action settings\n\n1. Ensure that a connection to your email is established (to establish a connection to the email module follow instructions in the Email documentation)\n\n2. Add recipients of the invitation in the To field\n\n3. Enter the subject of the email into the Subject field\n\n4. Add the Mustache module Compile a template action to the Content field\n\nThe result of our sample Mustache scenario:\nActivating a scenario\n\nOnce your Mustache scenario is tested and ready to use, you have to activate it.\n\nActivate your scenario by following Step 4 in the Creating a scenario article.\n\nMustache\nGetting Started with Mustache\nPrerequisites\nMustache\nAdding a Mustache Module to your Scenario\nTransformers\nCompile a Template\nSetting Up Variables in the Mustache Module\nSetting up a variable in the Mustache module\nSetting up a Target for the Mustache Template\nSend an email action settings\nActivating a scenario\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

\n\nDesktop flows extend the existing robotic process automation (RPA) capabilities in Power Automate and enable you to automate all repetitive desktop processes.\n\nItâs quicker and easier than ever to automate with the new, intuitive Power Automate desktop flow designer using the prebuilt drag-and-drop actions or recording your ownÂ desktop flowsÂ to run later.\n\nIn Power Automate, you can create flows,â¯interact with everyday tools such as email and Excel or work with modern and legacy applications. Some of the simple and complex tasks you can automate are:\n\norganize the documents using dedicated files and folders actions in less time\n\nextract data from websites accurately and store them in excel files using Web and Excel automation\n\nApply desktop automation capabilities to put your work on autopilot\n\nTo get started with Microsoft Power Automate, you need:\n\nMicrosoft Power Automate account\n\nAn Azure account to create custom apps\n\nConnect Microsoft Power Automate to Make\n\nYou can connect to Microsoft Power Automate in two ways:\n\nConnect using basic authentication\n\nConnect using OAuth credentials\n\nConnect using OAuth 2.0\n\nTo connect to Microsoft Power Automate:\n\nLog in to your Make , and open the Microsoft Power Automate module scenario .\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: In the MS PAD Environment ID field, enter your environment ID from your Power Automate account to which you want to connect.\n\nLeave this field empty to choose your default environment. If you have multiple environments, go to the Power Automate admin portalÂ to copy the desired environment ID.\n\nClick Continue.\n\nIn the pop-up window, enter your account details to sign in and authorize access by clicking Accept.\n\nYou have successfully connected the Microsoft Power Automate app and can now build scenarios .\n\nTo connect to Power Automate with your own credentials, you need to create a custom app in your Azure account and obtain the client credentials of the app.\n\nLog in to azure.portal.com.\n\nClick App Registrations.\n\nClick New Registration.\n\nEnter the details as provided in the table below and click Register.\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the app's name that you want to connect.\n\n\n\n\nSupported account types\n\n\t\n\nSelect the option, Accounts in any organizational directory (Any Azure AD Directory - Multitenant).\n\n\n\n\nRedirect URI (Optional)\n\n\t\n\nSelect the following options:\n\nPlatform: Web\n\nRedirect URI:\n\nhttps://auth.redirect.celonis.cloud/oauth/cb/microsoft-power-automate\n\nYou can find the Client ID and Tenant ID details on the app screen. To add a client secret, click Add a certificate or secret.\n\nClick New client secret. Enter a description and select the expiry period for the client secret. Click Add.\n\nCopy the Client Secret to a safe place.\n\nIn the Manifest section, change the allowPublicClient value to true, and click Save.\n\nLog in to your Make account and open the Microsoft Power Automate scenario , select the Advanced Settings checkbox.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nLeave this field empty to choose your default environment. If you have multiple environments, go to the Power Automate admin portalÂ to copy the desired environment ID.\n\nOptional: In the MS PAD Environment ID field, enter your environment ID from your Power Automate account to which you want to connect.\n\nIn the Client ID, Client Secret, and Tenant ID fields, enter the values copied in step 5 and step 7 respectively.\n\nClick Continue.\n\nIn the pop-up window, enter your account details to sign in and authorize access by clicking Accept.\n\nYou have all the details to connect your custom app with Make , and can now build scenarios .\n\nActions\n\nYou can run desktop flows using the following module.\n\nRun Desktop Flow\n\nSet up a desktop flow connection if you use the on-premises data gateway to trigger desktop flows.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Microsoft Power Automate account.\n\n\n\n\nSelect MS PAD Flow Connection\n\n\t\n\nEnter the connection flow ID of the desktop flow you want to run.\n\nTo create a flow connection, see connections.\n\nYou can get the Connection ID in your Power Automate account at Data > Connections > Select the connection > URL. In the URL address, find a part which says, ConnectionName and copy the ID that follows it\n\n\n\n\nSelect MS PAD Desktop Flow\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the flow you want to run. Only the Desktop Flows created in your Microsoft Power Automate account are displayed here.\n\nThe map function allows a user to map a value from one of the previous modules instead of selecting a Bot from the dropdown list.\n\nTo create a desktop flow, see UI flows.\n\n\n\n\nFlow Input fields\n\n\t\n\nAdd the input variables for the flow. These variables are passed to and from desktop flows, allowing you to create sophisticated flows.\n\nTo create variables, see input variables.\n\n\n\n\nSelect Run Mode\n\n\t\n\nSelect the run mode for the desktop flow depending on your settings.\n\nAttended: Requires an active Windows user session that matches the name of the user configured for your connection. The session must not be locked. When an attended desktop flow starts on the target machine, it is recommended to avoid interacting with your device until the run completes.\n\nUnattended: The target machine needs to be available with all users signed out. You cannot launch flows with elevated privileges.\n\nTo learn more about run modes, see desktop flow modes.\n\nFor more information on desktop flows, see Microsoft Power Automate documentation.\n\nMicrosoft Power Automate\nConnect Microsoft Power Automate to Make\nConnect using OAuth 2.0\nActions\nRun Desktop Flow\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

can insert, update, retrieve, search, and delete documents in your MongoDB account.\n\nTo use MongoDB modules, you must have a MongoDB account and a running instance of MongoDB configured for public access from the Internet. You will use this key in the API Token field in Make.\n\nLog in to yourÂ MakeÂ account, add aÂ Bubble module to yourÂ scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In theÂ Connection nameÂ field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nSelect either Application Domain or Custom Domain in the Domain Type field.\n\nIf you selected Application Domain, enter your Application Name. You can find this in your app's URL after id=. For example, if your app URL is https://bubble.io/page?name=index&amp;id=myapp-123&amp;tab=tabs-1), enter myapp-123.\n\nIf you selected Custom Domain, enter your Custom Domain URL. For example, https://www.yourcustomdomain.org).\n\nIn the API Token field, enter the Private key copied in Step 7.\n\nIn the Environment field, select if your app is in the Development (version-test) or Released (live) environment.\n\nClick Save.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. you to monitor repositories, users, or teams and create, update, retrieve, or delete issues, snippets, or milestones in your Bitbucket account.\n\nTo get started with Bitbucket, create an account at bitbucket.org.\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Bitbucket API documentation.\n\nConnecting Bitbucket to Make\n\nTo connect to the Bitbucket app:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add any Bitbucket module scenario, and click the Add button next to the Connection field.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show Advanced Settings and enter your custom app's Consumer Key and Secret values. See Bitbucket Oauth2.0 documentation.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, log in to your Bitbucket account and confirm the access by clicking the Grant Access button.\n\nYou have successfully connected the app and can now build scenarios.\n\nBuild Bitbucket Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nWatch a Repository\n\nCreates a new webhook on the specified repository.\n\nWatch a User\n\nCreates a new webhook on the specified user account. Account-level webhooks are fired for events from all repositories belonging to that account.\n\nNote\n\nOne can only register webhooks on one's own account and not that of others.\n\nWatch a Team\n\nCreates a new webhook on the specified team. Team webhooks are fired for events from all repositories belonging to that team account.\n\nNote\n\nOnly admins can install webhooks on teams.\n\nWatch a Workspace\n\nCreates a new webhook on the specified workspace.\n\nCreate an Issue\n\nCreates a new issue. Private repositories or issue trackers require the caller to authenticate with an account with appropriate authorization.\n\nGet an Issue\n\nReturns the specified issue.\n\nList Issues\n\nReturns the issues in the issue tracker.\n\nUpdate an Issue\n\nUpdates an issue.\n\nDelete an Issue\n\nDeletes the specified issue. This requires write access to the repository.\n\nCreate an Issue Comment\n\nCreates a new issue comment.\n\nList Milestones\n\nReturns the milestones that have been defined in the issue tracker. This resource is only available on repositories that have the issue tracker enabled.\n\nGet a Milestone\n\nReturns the specified issue tracker milestone object.\n\nList Repository Watchers\n\nReturns all watchers on the specified repository.\n\nGet a File\n\nReturns a redirect to the contents of a downloaded artifact. This endpoint returns the actual file contents and not the artifact's metadata.\n\nList Snippets\n\nReturns all snippets.\n\nGet a Snippet\n\nRetrieves a single snippet.\n\nStart Watching a Snippet\n\nStart watching a specific snippet.\n\nStop Watching a Snippet\n\nStops watching specific snippets.\n\nList Snippet Watchers\n\nReturns a list of all users watching a specific snippet.\n\nCreate a Snippet Comment\n\nCreates a new comment on a snippet.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nBitbucket\nConnecting Bitbucket to Make\nBuild Bitbucket Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You don't have to add authorization headers; we added those for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - Get Account Information\n\nThe following API call returns information about authenticated PrintNode account:\n\nURL:\n\n/v1/dashboard\n\nMethod:\n\nGET\n\nThe result can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body.\n\nIn our example, our account details were returned:\n\nPrintNode\nGetting Started with PrintNode\nConnecting PrintNode to Make\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Account Information\nPrev\nNext\nÂ© 2024 Celonis Inc."
